2943pub const SEVERITY_SUCCESS: HRESULT = 0;
2944pub const SEVERITY_ERROR: HRESULT = 1;
2945#[inline]
2946pub fn SUCCEEDED(hr: HRESULT) -> bool {
2947    hr >= 0
2948}
2949#[inline]
2950pub fn FAILED(hr: HRESULT) -> bool {
2951    hr < 0
2952}
2953#[inline]
2954pub fn IS_ERROR(hr: HRESULT) -> bool {
2955    (hr as u32) >> 31 == (SEVERITY_ERROR as u32)
2956}
2957#[inline]
2958pub fn HRESULT_CODE(hr: HRESULT) -> HRESULT {
2959    hr & 0xFFFF
2960}
2961#[inline]
2962pub fn SCODE_CODE(sc: SCODE) -> HRESULT {
2963    sc & 0xFFFF
2964}
2965#[inline]
2966pub fn HRESULT_FACILITY(hr: HRESULT) -> HRESULT {
2967    (hr >> 16) & 0x1fff
2968}
2969#[inline]
2970pub fn SCODE_FACILITY(sc: SCODE) -> HRESULT {
2971    (sc >> 16) & 0x1fff
2972}
2973#[inline]
2974pub fn HRESULT_SEVERITY(hr: HRESULT) -> HRESULT {
2975    (hr >> 31) & 0x1
2976}
2977#[inline]
2978pub fn SCODE_SEVERITY(sc: SCODE) -> HRESULT {
2979    (sc >> 31) & 0x1
2980}
2981#[inline]
2982pub fn MAKE_HRESULT(sev: HRESULT, fac: HRESULT, code: HRESULT) -> HRESULT {
2983    (sev << 31) | (fac << 16) | code
2984}
2985#[inline]
2986pub fn MAKE_SCODE(sev: HRESULT, fac: HRESULT, code: HRESULT) -> SCODE {
2987    (sev << 31) | (fac << 16) | code
2988}
2989pub const FACILITY_NT_BIT: HRESULT = 0x10000000;
2990#[inline]
2991pub fn HRESULT_FROM_WIN32(x: c_ulong) -> HRESULT {
2992    if x as i32 <= 0 {
2993        x as i32
2994    } else {
2995        ((x & 0x0000FFFF) | ((FACILITY_WIN32 as u32) << 16) | 0x80000000) as i32
2996    }
2997}
2998pub type HRESULT = c_long;
2999#[inline]
3000pub fn HRESULT_FROM_NT(x: c_ulong) -> HRESULT {
3001    (x | FACILITY_NT_BIT as u32) as i32
3002}
